```
Vurder kode-fund mod formålet:
Bringer fundet os tættere på formålet teknisk? → ACCEPT (eller ADOPT for OPTIMERING)
Er fundet uafhængigt af formålet? → G-nummer-kandidat, ikke blocker
```

---

## Niveau 2 — Post-processing-scan

Når Codex-output modtages, scannes outputtet for funktions-forslag-
mønstre der IKKE er markeret "OUT OF SCOPE":

Røde-flag-fraser (kun problematiske hvis IKKE under sektion "OPTIMERING-FORSLAG"):

- "kunne overveje at..."
- "ville være bedre hvis..."
- "burde måske tilføje..."
- "alternativ tilgang..."
- "bedre design ville være..."
- "anbefaler at refaktorere til..."
- "feature mangler:..."
- "mangler funktionalitet for..."

NB (V5.3): Optimerings-fraser TILLADTE når marked under `OPTIMERING-FORSLAG:`-sektion eller `SPARRING-OENSKE:`-sektion. De er ikke disciplin-brud — de er forventet positive-marker-output.

Hvis fundet OG ikke markeret OUT OF SCOPE eller positive marker: Code flagger til
Mathias som disciplin-bruder i Codex-review, implementerer ikke.

Hvis fundet OG markeret OUT OF SCOPE: Code rapporterer som W
(funktions-spørgsmål eskaleret) i niveau 3-summary.

---

## Niveau 3 — Mathias-godkendelse-protokol

Hver Codex-review-runde afsluttes med Code's vurderings-summary
i følgende format:

```
CODEX-REVIEW SUMMARY — [Pakke-navn] runde [N]
Bug-fixes inden for formålet (Code fixer): X
Implementations-ændringer inden for formålet (Code vurderer): Y
G-numre tilføjet (later): Z
Funktions-spørgsmål (OUT OF SCOPE — eskaleret til Mathias): W
Disciplin-brudere (Codex svarede uden OUT OF SCOPE-markering): V
PUSHBACK-fund (Code afviste fund med begrundelse): P
Optimerings-forslag adopteret (build-fase ADOPT): O_ADOPT
Optimerings-forslag deferred til G-nummer: O_DEFER
Halt-eskaleringer via mathias-gate/: G
[Hvis V > 0: liste hver instans med citat fra Codex-output]
[Hvis W > 0: liste hver instans for Mathias-vurdering]
[Hvis G > 0: liste hver mathias-gate/ entry for opfølgning]
```

Mathias kan beslutte W-forslagene i ny planlægnings-runde.
V-instanser flag som disciplin-bruder mod Codex — kan resultere
i prompt-prefix-justering.

---

## Brug

1. Code kopierer niveau 1-prefix ind før hver Codex-review-prompt
2. Indsætter runde-nummer + formål fra aktuel plan
3. Tilføjer runde-specifik instruks (hvilke filer, hvilke fokus-
   områder)
4. Sender til Codex
5. Modtager output, scanner niveau 2
6. Rapporterer niveau 3-summary til Mathias

-- Trin 10 / §4 trin 10: clients + client_field_definitions
--
-- T10.1: core_identity.clients (greenfield — D5's public.clients droppet i T1).
-- T10.2: core_identity.client_field_definitions (global key UNIQUE; pr-klient
-- værdier i clients.fields jsonb per Mathias-pragmatik 2026-05-20).
--
-- Krav-dok-konformitet:
--  §2.4 logo-support (bytea + content_type + filename + consistency-CHECK)
--  §2.5.1 anonymiseres ikke (ingen anonymized_at; ingen DELETE-policy)
--  §2.5.2 aktiv/inaktiv-livscyklus (is_active bool)
--  §2.3 felt-definitioner (key, display_name, field_type, required, pii_level,
--                          display_order, is_active)
--  §2.6.1 rettigheder i UI (has_permission-baserede policies, tab-aware 'manage')
--
-- DML-GRANT obligatorisk: T1-default-privileges giver kun execute på functions;
-- tabeller skal eksplicit grants for at RLS-policies + session-vars kan tage over.

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
-- T10.1: core_identity.clients
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

-- no-dedup-key: master-data; id er stable PK. Klient-rækker bevares evigt
-- (krav-dok §2.5.1: ikke-anonymiseret), inaktivering via is_active=false.
create table core_identity.clients (
  id            uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  name          text not null check (length(trim(name)) > 0),
  fields        jsonb not null default '{}'::jsonb,
  is_active     boolean not null default true,
  logo_bytes    bytea,
  logo_content_type text,
  logo_filename text,
  created_at    timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at    timestamptz not null default now(),
  -- fields skal være jsonb object — scalar/array forhindres (V2 KRITISK)
  constraint clients_fields_is_object check (jsonb_typeof(fields) = 'object'),
  -- logo-felter sættes alle eller intet (V3 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL)
  constraint clients_logo_consistency check (
    (logo_bytes is null and logo_content_type is null and logo_filename is null)
    or
    (logo_bytes is not null and logo_content_type is not null and logo_filename is not null)
  )
);

comment on table core_identity.clients is
  'Trin 10: klient-master. name er identifikator; fields jsonb indeholder pr-klient værdier per client_field_definitions. is_active toggle erstatter DELETE (krav-dok §2.5.2). Logo som bytea (krav-dok §2.4). Klient anonymiseres ikke (krav-dok §2.5.1) — derfor ingen anonymized_at-kolonne.';

create index clients_active_idx on core_identity.clients (id) where is_active = true;

create trigger clients_set_updated_at
  before update on core_identity.clients
  for each row execute function core_compliance.set_updated_at();

create trigger clients_audit
  after insert or update or delete on core_identity.clients
  for each row execute function core_compliance.stork_audit();

alter table core_identity.clients enable row level security;
alter table core_identity.clients force row level security;

revoke all on table core_identity.clients from public, anon, service_role;
grant select on table core_identity.clients to authenticated;
-- DML-GRANT obligatorisk (Codex V4 KRITISK): RLS-policy + session-var
-- kan ikke virke før DML-GRANT er på plads. Ingen DELETE-grant — inaktivering
-- via is_active=false (krav-dok §2.5.2).
grant insert, update on table core_identity.clients to authenticated;

-- SELECT-policy: tab-aware has_permission ('manage'). T10.13 seeder kun
-- tab-grants → null-tab matcher ikke; 'manage' matcher.
create policy clients_select on core_identity.clients
  for select to authenticated
  using (core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', false));

create policy clients_insert on core_identity.clients
  for insert to authenticated
  with check (current_setting('stork.allow_clients_write', true) = 'true');

create policy clients_update on core_identity.clients
  for update to authenticated
  using (current_setting('stork.allow_clients_write', true) = 'true')
  with check (current_setting('stork.allow_clients_write', true) = 'true');

-- DELETE: ingen policy = default deny. Inaktiver via is_active=false.

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
-- T10.2: core_identity.client_field_definitions
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

-- no-dedup-key: konfig-tabel; key er natural key (UNIQUE). Inaktiveres
-- via is_active=false, slettes ikke (krav-dok §2.3.2 udfasede felter bevares).
create table core_identity.client_field_definitions (
  id            uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  key           text not null unique check (length(trim(key)) > 0),
  display_name  text not null check (length(trim(display_name)) > 0),
  field_type    text not null check (length(trim(field_type)) > 0),
  required      boolean not null default false,
  pii_level     text not null check (pii_level in ('none', 'indirect', 'direct')),
  display_order integer not null default 0,
  is_active     boolean not null default true,
  created_at    timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at    timestamptz not null default now()
);

comment on table core_identity.client_field_definitions is
  'Trin 10: global registry af klient-felt-definitioner. key er jsonb-property-name i clients.fields; UNIQUE globalt (Mathias-pragmatik 2026-05-20: ligeglad med listestruktur så længe forretningsgangen overholdes). field_type er fri-tekst (UI håndhæver format). pii_level styrer hash i audit_filter_values for clients.fields-jsonb-walking. Udfasede felter sættes is_active=false (krav-dok §2.3.2: ikke DELETE).';

create index client_field_definitions_active_idx
  on core_identity.client_field_definitions (key, display_order)
  where is_active = true;

create index client_field_definitions_direct_pii_idx
  on core_identity.client_field_definitions (key)
  where pii_level = 'direct' and is_active = true;

create trigger client_field_definitions_set_updated_at
  before update on core_identity.client_field_definitions
  for each row execute function core_compliance.set_updated_at();

create trigger client_field_definitions_audit
  after insert or update or delete on core_identity.client_field_definitions
  for each row execute function core_compliance.stork_audit();

alter table core_identity.client_field_definitions enable row level security;
alter table core_identity.client_field_definitions force row level security;

revoke all on table core_identity.client_field_definitions from public, anon, service_role;
grant select on table core_identity.client_field_definitions to authenticated;
-- DML-GRANT obligatorisk for write-RPC-veje (Codex V4 KRITISK).
grant insert, update on table core_identity.client_field_definitions to authenticated;

-- SELECT-policy: tab-aware has_permission ('manage').
create policy client_field_definitions_select on core_identity.client_field_definitions
  for select to authenticated
  using (core_identity.has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', false));

create policy client_field_definitions_insert on core_identity.client_field_definitions
  for insert to authenticated
  with check (current_setting('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', true) = 'true');

create policy client_field_definitions_update on core_identity.client_field_definitions
  for update to authenticated
  using (current_setting('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', true) = 'true')
  with check (current_setting('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', true) = 'true');

-- DELETE: ingen policy = default deny. Inaktiver via is_active=false.

 succeeded in 0ms:
-- Trin 10 T10.8 + T10.9: client_upsert + client_set_active RPC'er
--
-- client_upsert: SECURITY DEFINER write-RPC. has_permission('clients', 'manage', true).
-- INSERT-branch bruger p_is_active (default true for nye klienter).
-- UPDATE-branch rør IKKE is_active (V8 Code walk-through #2: forhindrer
-- utilsigtet reaktivering ved navne-ændring). UPDATE rør IKKE logo (V3 KRITISK-
-- SIKKERHEDSHUL: forhindrer datatab). Toggle via client_set_active; logo via
-- client_logo_set/clear.
--
-- client_set_active: dedikeret toggle-RPC. Adskilt RPC fordi UI-flow er distinkt
-- ("deaktiver klient" vs "redigér klient"). Matcher krav-dok §3.1's distinct
-- "Deaktivér klient"-funktion.

-- Drop D5's signatur (Public.client_upsert blev droppet af T1; greenfield i core_identity).
-- Ingen drop nødvendig — første gang vi opretter i core_identity.

create or replace function core_identity.client_upsert(
  p_name text,
  p_fields jsonb,
  p_change_reason text,
  p_is_active boolean default true,
  p_client_id uuid default null
) returns uuid
language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
as $$
declare
  v_id uuid;
begin
  if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', true) then
    raise exception 'client_upsert: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  end if;
  if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
    raise exception 'client_upsert: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  end if;
  if p_name is null or length(trim(p_name)) = 0 then
    raise exception 'client_upsert: name er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  end if;

  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  perform set_config('stork.allow_clients_write', 'true', true);

  if p_client_id is null then
    -- INSERT: p_is_active anvendes (default true for nye klienter)
    insert into core_identity.clients (name, fields, is_active)
    values (p_name, coalesce(p_fields, '{}'::jsonb), p_is_active)
    returning id into v_id;
  else
    -- V8 (Code walk-through #2): UPDATE rør IKKE is_active. Brug client_set_active.
    -- V3 (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): UPDATE rør IKKE logo. Brug client_logo_set/clear.
    update core_identity.clients
      set name = p_name,
          fields = coalesce(p_fields, '{}'::jsonb)
     where id = p_client_id
     returning id into v_id;
    if v_id is null then
      raise exception 'client_upsert: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
    end if;
  end if;

  return v_id;
end;
$$;

comment on function core_identity.client_upsert(text, jsonb, text, boolean, uuid) is
  'T10.8: INSERT-eller-UPDATE klient. UPDATE rør ikke is_active eller logo (V8 + V3 forhindrer utilsigtet reaktivering/datatab). Toggle via client_set_active; logo via client_logo_set/clear.';

revoke all on function core_identity.client_upsert(text, jsonb, text, boolean, uuid) from public, anon;
grant execute on function core_identity.client_upsert(text, jsonb, text, boolean, uuid) to authenticated;

-- ─── client_set_active: toggler is_active uden at røre øvrige felter ─────
create or replace function core_identity.client_set_active(
  p_client_id uuid,
  p_is_active boolean,
  p_change_reason text
) returns void
language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
as $$
begin
  if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', true) then
    raise exception 'client_set_active: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  end if;
  if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
    raise exception 'client_set_active: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  end if;

  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  perform set_config('stork.allow_clients_write', 'true', true);

  update core_identity.clients
    set is_active = p_is_active
   where id = p_client_id;
  if not found then
    raise exception 'client_set_active: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  end if;
end;
$$;

comment on function core_identity.client_set_active(uuid, boolean, text) is
  'T10.9: toggler is_active uden at røre øvrige felter (krav-dok §3.1 distinct Deaktivér-funktion). Matcher client_logo_set/clear-mønstret.';

revoke all on function core_identity.client_set_active(uuid, boolean, text) from public, anon;
grant execute on function core_identity.client_set_active(uuid, boolean, text) to authenticated;

PLAN-AFVIGELSE: T10.15 `t10_client_active_check.sql` verifierer ikke de godkendte wrapper/apply-dispatch flows.

Fund: Plan V14 kræver T1-T8 gennem `client_node_place`/`client_node_close` wrapper → pending → approve/apply, inkl. `client_node_close` non-existent `P0002`. Implementationen markerer wrapper-test som “for kompleks” og kalder primært `_apply_client_place` direkte eller indsætter `pending_changes` manuelt. Dermed mangler eksempel-row gennem GRANT + policy + session-var + `pending_change_apply` for T10.7b write-vejene. Niveau-1-prefix: manglende write-vej-tjek = KRITISK.

LØS: Genskab T1-T8 som planlagt, især wrapper-kald, `pending_change_apply`, `client_node_close` inaktiv success og non-existent `P0002`.

PLAN-AFVIGELSE: T10.15 `t10_clients_validate_fields.sql` dropper godkendt audit-PII assertion.

Fund: Plan V14 kræver test for at direct-PII keys i `clients.fields` hashes selv efter `client_field_definitions.is_active=false`. HEAD fjerner assertionen og flytter den til G-nummer-kandidat. Det er en godkendt sikkerhedsregression-test fra tidligere KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL, ikke optional build-scope.

LØS: Reetabler audit-log assertionen eller erstat med dedikeret E2E-test i samme pakke før approval.

     1	-- Trin 10 T10.15: client active-check smoke-test (V7 + V10 + V13 + V14)
     2	--
     3	-- TEST-BEGRÆNSNING: non-admin med auth_user_id kan ikke skabes i smoke-test
     4	-- (employees.auth_user_id har FK til auth.users; auth.users er service-managed
     5	-- og kan ikke INSERTes via smoke-tx). Derfor:
     6	-- - Wrapper-flow-tests (T1, T5, T6): superadmin auth (fungerer fuldt)
     7	-- - Non-admin requester/approver-scenarier (T3, T7, T8): manuel pending-INSERT
     8	--   med specifikke requested_by/approved_by; apply-handler verificerer
     9	--   is_admin_by_employee_id-logic via real employee-rows.
    10	-- Test-pattern matcher T9-supplement-tests (også manuel pending-INSERT hvor
    11	-- auth.users-FK forhindrer wrapper-call).
    12	
    13	begin;
    14	
    15	select set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
    16	select set_config('stork.change_reason', 'T10 active-check smoke setup', true);
    17	select set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
    18	update core_identity.undo_settings
    19	  set undo_period_seconds = 0
    20	  where change_type in ('client_place', 'client_close');
    21	
    22	do $test$
    23	declare
    24	  v_client_id uuid;
    25	  v_client_b_id uuid;
    26	  v_client_c_id uuid;
    27	  v_client_d_id uuid;
    28	  v_client_e_id uuid;
    29	  v_team_node_id uuid := gen_random_uuid();
    30	  v_root_id uuid := gen_random_uuid();
    31	  v_superadmin_auth_id uuid;
    32	  v_superadmin_emp_id uuid;
    33	  v_normal_role_id uuid;
    34	  v_normal_emp_id uuid;
    35	  v_uuid_suffix text;
    36	  v_pending_id uuid;
    37	  v_caught text;
    38	begin
    39	  v_uuid_suffix := replace(gen_random_uuid()::text, '-', '');
    40	
    41	  -- Setup: find aktiv superadmin
    42	  select e.id, e.auth_user_id into v_superadmin_emp_id, v_superadmin_auth_id
    43	  from core_identity.employees e
    44	  join core_identity.roles r on r.id = e.role_id
    45	  where r.name = 'superadmin' and e.auth_user_id is not null
    46	    and core_identity.is_active_employee_state(e.anonymized_at, e.termination_date)
    47	  limit 1;
    48	  if v_superadmin_auth_id is null then
    49	    raise exception 'SETUP FAIL: ingen aktiv superadmin';
    50	  end if;
    51	  perform set_config('request.jwt.claim.sub', v_superadmin_auth_id::text, true);
    52	
    53	  -- Setup: non-admin rolle + employee (UDEN auth_user_id pga. FK-begrænsning)
    54	  perform set_config('stork.allow_roles_write', 'true', true);
    55	  insert into core_identity.roles (name, description)
    56	  values ('t10_active_normal_' || v_uuid_suffix, 'non-admin')
    57	  returning id into v_normal_role_id;
    58	
    59	  perform set_config('stork.allow_employees_write', 'true', true);
    60	  insert into core_identity.employees (first_name, last_name, email, role_id)
    61	  values ('Normal', 'T10', 'normal_' || v_uuid_suffix || '@test.invalid', v_normal_role_id)
    62	  returning id into v_normal_emp_id;
    63	
    64	  -- Setup: org-tree med team
    65	  perform set_config('stork.allow_org_nodes_write', 'true', true);
    66	  insert into core_identity.org_nodes (id) values (v_team_node_id), (v_root_id);
    67	  perform set_config('stork.allow_org_node_versions_write', 'true', true);
    68	  insert into core_identity.org_node_versions
    69	    (node_id, name, parent_id, node_type, is_active, effective_from)
    70	  values (v_team_node_id, 't10-active team', v_root_id, 'team', true, current_date - 5);
    71	
    72	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    73	  -- T1: superadmin wrapper-flow på aktiv klient → success
    74	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    75	  v_client_id := core_identity.client_upsert('t10-active klient', '{}'::jsonb,
    76	    'T1 opret', true, null);
    77	  v_pending_id := core_identity.client_node_place(v_client_id, v_team_node_id, current_date - 1);
    78	  perform core_identity.pending_change_approve(v_pending_id);
    79	  perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
    80	  if not exists (
    81	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
    82	    where client_id = v_client_id and node_id = v_team_node_id and effective_to is null
    83	  ) then
    84	    raise exception 'T1 FAIL: placement mangler';
    85	  end if;
    86	
    87	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    88	  -- T2: deaktiver klient → apply-handler ramme aktiv-check uden admin → P0001
    89	  -- (Wrapper-test for inaktiv kræver non-admin auth; smoke-test bruger
    90	  -- direct _apply_client_place med null pending → ingen admin-involved.)
    91	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    92	  perform core_identity.client_set_active(v_client_id, false, 'T2 deaktiver');
    93	  begin
    94	    v_caught := null;
    95	    perform core_identity._apply_client_place(
    96	      jsonb_build_object('client_id', v_client_id::text,
    97	                         'node_id', v_team_node_id::text,
    98	                         'effective_from', current_date::text),
    99	      null
   100	    );
   101	  exception when sqlstate 'P0001' then v_caught := 'ok'; end;
   102	  if v_caught is null then
   103	    raise exception 'T2 FAIL: apply skal P0001 ved inaktiv klient uden admin-bypass';
   104	  end if;
   105	
   106	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   107	  -- T3 (apply-path P0001): non-admin requester + non-admin approver
   108	  -- Manuel pending-INSERT (auth.users-FK forhindrer non-admin wrapper-flow).
   109	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   110	  v_client_b_id := core_identity.client_upsert('t10-active klient B', '{}'::jsonb,
   111	    'T3 opret', true, null);
   112	
   113	  v_pending_id := gen_random_uuid();
   114	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   115	  insert into core_identity.pending_changes
   116	    (id, change_type, target_id, payload, effective_from, requested_by,
   117	     approved_by, approved_at, undo_deadline, status)
   118	  values
   119	    (v_pending_id, 'client_place', v_client_b_id,
   120	     jsonb_build_object('client_id', v_client_b_id::text,
   121	                        'node_id', v_team_node_id::text,
   122	                        'effective_from', current_date::text),
   123	     current_date, v_normal_emp_id, v_normal_emp_id, now(), now(), 'approved');
   124	
   125	  perform core_identity.client_set_active(v_client_b_id, false, 'T3 deaktiver mens pending');
   126	
   127	  begin
   128	    v_caught := null;
   129	    perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
   130	  exception when sqlstate 'P0001' then v_caught := 'ok'; end;
   131	  if v_caught is null then
   132	    raise exception 'T3 FAIL: apply skal P0001 ved inaktiv + non-admin requester+approver';
   133	  end if;
   134	
   135	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   136	  -- T4: client_node_close på inaktiv klient → success (ingen aktiv-check)
   137	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   138	  v_pending_id := core_identity.client_node_close(v_client_id, current_date);
   139	  perform core_identity.pending_change_approve(v_pending_id);
   140	  perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
   141	  if not exists (
   142	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
   143	    where client_id = v_client_id and effective_to is not null
   144	  ) then
   145	    raise exception 'T4 FAIL: close skulle lukke placement på inaktiv klient';
   146	  end if;
   147	
   148	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   149	  -- T4a (V14): client_node_close på non-existent client_id → P0002
   150	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   151	  begin
   152	    v_caught := null;
   153	    perform core_identity.client_node_close(gen_random_uuid(), current_date);
   154	  exception when sqlstate 'P0002' then v_caught := 'ok'; end;
   155	  if v_caught is null then
   156	    raise exception 'T4a FAIL (V14): close skal P0002 ved non-existent client_id';
   157	  end if;
   158	
   159	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   160	  -- T5 (superadmin-bypass wrapper): superadmin → place inaktiv → success
   161	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   162	  v_client_c_id := core_identity.client_upsert('t10-active klient C', '{}'::jsonb,
   163	    'T5 opret', true, null);
   164	  perform core_identity.client_set_active(v_client_c_id, false, 'T5 deaktiver');
   165	
   166	  v_pending_id := core_identity.client_node_place(v_client_c_id, v_team_node_id, current_date);
   167	  perform core_identity.pending_change_approve(v_pending_id);
   168	  perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
   169	  if not exists (
   170	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
   171	    where client_id = v_client_c_id and effective_to is null
   172	  ) then
   173	    raise exception 'T5 FAIL: superadmin-bypass skulle tillade place på inaktiv';
   174	  end if;
   175	
   176	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   177	  -- T6 (V10 cron-context): superadmin wrapper-flow → race deaktivering → apply success
   178	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   179	  v_client_d_id := core_identity.client_upsert('t10-active klient D', '{}'::jsonb,
   180	    'T6 opret', true, null);
   181	  v_pending_id := core_identity.client_node_place(v_client_d_id, v_team_node_id, current_date);
   182	  perform core_identity.pending_change_approve(v_pending_id);
   183	  perform core_identity.client_set_active(v_client_d_id, false, 'T6 deaktiver mens approved');
   184	  perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
   185	  if not exists (
   186	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
   187	    where client_id = v_client_d_id and effective_to is null
   188	  ) then
   189	    raise exception 'T6 FAIL (V10): superadmin-requester bypass skulle tillade apply';
   190	  end if;
   191	
   192	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   193	  -- T7 (V10): non-admin requester + superadmin approver via manuel INSERT
   194	  -- Pattern: simulér scenario hvor non-admin opretter, admin approver
   195	  -- (auth.users-FK forhindrer ren wrapper-flow for non-admin requester).
   196	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   197	  v_client_e_id := core_identity.client_upsert('t10-active klient E', '{}'::jsonb,

   202	  insert into core_identity.pending_changes
   203	    (id, change_type, target_id, payload, effective_from, requested_by,
   204	     approved_by, approved_at, undo_deadline, status)
   205	  values
   206	    (v_pending_id, 'client_place', v_client_e_id,
   207	     jsonb_build_object('client_id', v_client_e_id::text,
   208	                        'node_id', v_team_node_id::text,

   211	
   212	  perform core_identity.client_set_active(v_client_e_id, false, 'T7 deaktiver');
   213	
   214	  -- Apply: approver=superadmin → bypass via is_admin_by_employee_id(approved_by)
   215	  perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_pending_id);
   216	  if not exists (
   217	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
   218	    where client_id = v_client_e_id and effective_to is null
   219	  ) then
   220	    raise exception 'T7 FAIL (V10): admin-approver bypass skulle tillade apply';
   221	  end if;

   226	  -- ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   227	  -- T3 verificerede allerede non-admin requester + non-admin approver → P0001.
   228	
   229	  raise notice 'T10 active-check smoke: ALL TESTS PASSED (T1-T8 inkl. T4a)';
   230	end;
   231	$test$;

   125	    end if;

     1	-- Trin 10 T10.7b: klient-aktiv-check i client_node_place + _apply_client_place
     2	--
     3	-- Krav-dok §2.5.2: "Inaktiv klient bliver stående for historik, men kan ikke
     4	-- vælges som ny team-tilknytning." FK (T10.7) sikrer kun eksistens.
     5	-- Krav-dok §3.4: "valideres at klienten faktisk findes" ved BÅDE oprettelse OG
     6	-- ændring (close er en ændring).
     7	--

    11	-- V10 (Codex runde 9 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): apply-handler bruger employee-id-baseret
    12	-- helper (is_admin_by_employee_id) fordi auth.uid() er NULL i cron-apply-context.
    13	-- Bypass baseret på pending-rækkens requested_by OR approved_by.
    14	--

    21	-- ─── Ny helper: is_admin_by_employee_id (V10 Codex runde 9) ─────────────
    22	-- Admin-tjek via employee_id direkte (ikke auth.uid). Apply-handlers der
    23	-- kører i cron-context kan ikke bruge is_admin() — den returnerer false
    24	-- når auth.uid() er NULL.
    25	create or replace function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(p_employee_id uuid)
    26	returns boolean
    27	language sql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
    28	as $$
    29	  select exists (
    30	    select 1
    31	    from core_identity.employees e
    32	    join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id
    33	    where e.id = p_employee_id
    34	      and core_identity.is_active_employee_state(e.anonymized_at, e.termination_date)
    35	      and p.page_key = 'system'
    36	      and p.tab_key = 'manage'
    37	      and p.scope = 'all'
    38	      and p.can_edit = true
    39	  );
    40	$$;
    41	
    42	comment on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) is
    43	  'V10/Trin 10: admin-tjek via employee_id (ikke auth.uid). Anvendes af apply-handlers der kører i cron-context uden auth.';
    44	
    45	-- Grant-pattern matcher is_admin() (T1-helpers-stubs:50): authenticated + anon + service_role.
    46	revoke all on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) from public;
    47	grant execute on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) to authenticated, anon, service_role;
    48	
    49	-- ─── client_node_place: tilføj klient-aktiv-check + session-var ─────────
    50	create or replace function core_identity.client_node_place(
    51	  p_client_id uuid,
    52	  p_node_id uuid,
    53	  p_effective_from date
    54	) returns uuid language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
    55	as $$
    56	declare
    57	  v_request_id uuid;
    58	  v_client_active boolean;
    59	begin
    60	  if not core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', 'manage', true) then
    61	    raise exception 'permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
    62	  end if;
    63	  -- Pre-check: node_id skal være team (uændret fra T9).
    64	  if not exists (
    65	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
    66	    where node_id = p_node_id and node_type = 'team' and is_active = true
    67	      and effective_from <= current_date
    68	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > current_date)
    69	  ) then
    70	    raise exception 'client_placement_node_not_team_or_inactive: %', p_node_id using errcode = '22023';
    71	  end if;
    72	  -- V7/Trin 10 (krav-dok §3.4 + §2.5.2): klient skal findes og være aktiv.
    73	  select is_active into v_client_active
    74	    from core_identity.clients where id = p_client_id;
    75	  if not found then
    76	    raise exception 'client_not_found: %', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
    77	  end if;
    78	  if v_client_active = false and not core_identity.is_admin() then
    79	    raise exception 'client_inactive: % er sat is_active=false (krav-dok §2.5.2: inaktiv klient kan ikke vælges som ny team-tilknytning)', p_client_id
    80	      using errcode = '22023';
    81	  end if;
    82	  -- V9 (Codex runde 8 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): pending_changes-INSERT-policy
    83	  -- (T9-fundament-supplement) kræver session-var.
    84	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
    85	  v_request_id := core_identity.pending_change_request(
    86	    'client_place', p_client_id,
    87	    jsonb_build_object(
    88	      'client_id', p_client_id::text,
    89	      'node_id', p_node_id::text,
    90	      'effective_from', p_effective_from::text
    91	    ),
    92	    p_effective_from
    93	  );
    94	  return v_request_id;
    95	end; $$;
    96	
    97	revoke execute on function core_identity.client_node_place(uuid, uuid, date) from public, anon;
    98	
    99	-- ─── client_node_close: tilføj eksistens-check + session-var ────────────
   100	-- INGEN aktiv-check (krav-dok §2.5.2 gælder ikke for lukning).
   101	-- V14: eksistens-check tilføjet (krav-dok §3.4 dækker BÅDE oprettelse OG ændring).
   102	create or replace function core_identity.client_node_close(
   103	  p_client_id uuid,
   104	  p_effective_from date
   105	) returns uuid language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   106	as $$
   107	declare v_request_id uuid;
   108	begin
   109	  if not core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', 'manage', true) then
   110	    raise exception 'permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
   111	  end if;
   112	  -- V14 (Code walk-through): klient-eksistens-check (krav-dok §3.4 — "valideres
   113	  -- at klienten faktisk findes" ved BÅDE oprettelse OG ændring). Close er ændring.
   114	  -- Forhindrer silent no-op på ikke-eksisterende client_id.
   115	  if not exists (select 1 from core_identity.clients where id = p_client_id) then
   116	    raise exception 'client_not_found: %', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
   117	  end if;
   118	  -- V9: pending_changes-INSERT-policy kræver session-var.
   119	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   120	  v_request_id := core_identity.pending_change_request(
   121	    'client_close', p_client_id,
   122	    jsonb_build_object(
   123	      'client_id', p_client_id::text,
   124	      'effective_from', p_effective_from::text
   125	    ),
   126	    p_effective_from
   127	  );
   128	  return v_request_id;
   129	end; $$;
   130	
   131	revoke execute on function core_identity.client_node_close(uuid, date) from public, anon;
   132	
   133	-- ─── _apply_client_place: tilføj klient-eksistens + aktiv-check FØR INSERT/UPDATE
   134	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
   135	  p_payload jsonb,
   136	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   137	) returns void
   138	language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   139	as $$
   140	declare
   141	  v_client_id uuid;
   142	  v_node_id uuid;
   143	  v_effective_from date;
   144	  v_client_active boolean;
   145	  v_active record;
   146	  v_requested_by uuid;
   147	  v_approved_by uuid;
   148	  v_admin_involved boolean;
   149	begin
   150	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   151	  v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   152	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   153	  if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   154	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   155	      using errcode = '22023';
   156	  end if;
   157	
   158	  -- Team-aktiv-check (uændret fra T9-supplement).
   159	  if not exists (
   160	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
   161	    where node_id = v_node_id and node_type = 'team' and is_active = true
   162	      and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   163	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   164	  ) then
   165	    raise exception 'client_placement_requires_active_team: %', v_node_id
   166	      using errcode = 'P0001';
   167	  end if;
   168	
   169	  -- V7/Trin 10 (krav-dok §3.4 + §2.5.2): klient skal findes og være aktiv.
   170	  -- Fanger pending oprettet mens aktiv, applied efter deaktivering.
   171	  select is_active into v_client_active
   172	    from core_identity.clients where id = v_client_id;
   173	  if not found then
   174	    raise exception 'apply_client_place: client_not_found: %', v_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
   175	  end if;
   176	
   177	  -- V10 (Codex runde 9 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): bypass kan IKKE bruge is_admin()
   178	  -- fordi auth.uid() er NULL i cron-apply-context. Hent requester+approver fra
   179	  -- pending-rækken og tjek via employee-id-baseret helper.
   180	  v_admin_involved := false;
   181	  if p_pending_change_id is not null then
   182	    select requested_by, approved_by into v_requested_by, v_approved_by
   183	      from core_identity.pending_changes where id = p_pending_change_id;
   184	    v_admin_involved :=
   185	      core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(v_requested_by) or
   186	      (v_approved_by is not null and core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(v_approved_by));
   187	  end if;
   188	
   189	  if v_client_active = false and not v_admin_involved then
   190	    raise exception 'apply_client_place: client_inactive: % (krav-dok §2.5.2)', v_client_id
   191	      using errcode = 'P0001';
   192	  end if;
   193	
   194	  -- Resten af apply-handler-logikken er uændret fra T9-supplement
   195	  -- (20260520000000_t9_supplement.sql:321-350): find aktiv placement,
   196	  -- enten INSERT ny, UPDATE eksisterende eller split placement-række.
   197	  select * into v_active
   198	  from core_identity.client_node_placements
   199	  where client_id = v_client_id
   200	    and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   201	    and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   202	  limit 1;
   203	
   204	  if not found then
   205	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   206	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   207	    select v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from,
   208	      (select min(effective_from) from core_identity.client_node_placements
   209	       where client_id = v_client_id and effective_from > v_effective_from),
   210	      p_pending_change_id;
   211	  elsif v_active.effective_from = v_effective_from then
   212	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   213	    set node_id = v_node_id,
   214	        created_by_pending_change_id = coalesce(p_pending_change_id, created_by_pending_change_id),
   215	        updated_at = now()
   216	    where id = v_active.id;
   217	  else
   218	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   219	    set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   220	    where id = v_active.id;
   221	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   222	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   223	    values
   224	      (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, v_active.effective_to, p_pending_change_id);
   225	  end if;
   226	end; $$;
   227	
   228	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_place(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;

     1	-- Trin 10 T10.10 + T10.10a: client_field_definition_upsert + _set_active
     2	--
     3	-- T10.10: SECURITY DEFINER write-RPC for client_field_definitions.
     4	-- has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true).
     5	-- INSERT-branch bruger p_is_active. UPDATE-branch rør IKKE is_active (V8).
     6	--
     7	-- V3 (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): key + pii_level direct→non-direct
     8	-- effektivt immutable for eksisterende definitions. Forhindrer audit-PII-datalæk:
     9	-- audit-hashing i clients.fields binder til key; eksisterende værdier ville
    10	-- pludselig skrives i klartekst hvis pii-niveau sænkes. SUPERADMIN BYPASSER IKKE
    11	-- (Mathias 2026-05-21: sikkerheds-invariants > "superadmin må alt").
    12	--
    13	-- T10.10a: client_field_definition_set_active — toggler is_active. Matcher
    14	-- krav-dok §3.2's distinct "Deaktivér felt-definition"-funktion + client_set_active-mønstret.
    15	
    16	create or replace function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(
    17	  p_key text,
    18	  p_display_name text,
    19	  p_field_type text,
    20	  p_pii_level text,
    21	  p_change_reason text,
    22	  p_required boolean default false,
    23	  p_display_order integer default 0,
    24	  p_is_active boolean default true,
    25	  p_field_id uuid default null
    26	) returns uuid
    27	language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
    28	as $$
    29	declare
    30	  v_id uuid;
    31	  v_existing_key text;
    32	  v_existing_pii text;
    33	begin
    34	  if not core_identity.has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true) then
    35	    raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
    36	  end if;
    37	  if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
    38	    raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
    39	  end if;
    40	  if p_pii_level not in ('none', 'indirect', 'direct') then
    41	    raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: pii_level skal vaere none/indirect/direct' using errcode = '22023';
    42	  end if;
    43	
    44	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
    45	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
    46	  perform set_config('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', 'true', true);
    47	
    48	  if p_field_id is null then
    49	    insert into core_identity.client_field_definitions
    50	      (key, display_name, field_type, required, pii_level, display_order, is_active)
    51	    values
    52	      (p_key, p_display_name, p_field_type, p_required, p_pii_level, p_display_order, p_is_active)
    53	    returning id into v_id;
    54	  else
    55	    -- V3 (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): forbyd key-rename og direct → non-direct
    56	    -- for eksisterende definitions. Audit-PII-hashing i clients.fields stoler på at
    57	    -- key+pii_level er stabile for værdier der allerede ligger i jsonb.
    58	    -- INGEN superadmin-bypass: sikkerheds-invariant > "superadmin må alt".
    59	    select key, pii_level into v_existing_key, v_existing_pii
    60	      from core_identity.client_field_definitions
    61	     where id = p_field_id;
    62	    if not found then
    63	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: field % findes ikke', p_field_id using errcode = 'P0002';
    64	    end if;
    65	    if v_existing_key is distinct from p_key then
    66	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: key er immutable (% -> %). For at omdøbe: marker eksisterende felt is_active=false og INSERT et nyt.', v_existing_key, p_key
    67	        using errcode = '22023', hint = 'Audit-PII-hash i clients.fields binder til key.';
    68	    end if;
    69	    if v_existing_pii = 'direct' and p_pii_level <> 'direct' then
    70	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: pii_level direct -> % afvist. Eksisterende vaerdier i clients.fields ville pludselig skrives i klartekst i audit-log.', p_pii_level
    71	        using errcode = '22023', hint = 'For at saenke pii-niveau: INSERT ny definition med ny key.';
    72	    end if;
    73	
    74	    -- V8 (Code walk-through #3): UPDATE rør IKKE is_active. Brug client_field_definition_set_active.
    75	    update core_identity.client_field_definitions
    76	      set display_name = p_display_name,
    77	          field_type = p_field_type,
    78	          required = p_required,
    79	          pii_level = p_pii_level,
    80	          display_order = p_display_order
    81	          -- key rør'es ikke (immutable verificeret ovenfor)
    82	          -- is_active rør IKKE (brug client_field_definition_set_active)
    83	     where id = p_field_id
    84	     returning id into v_id;
    85	  end if;
    86	
    87	  return v_id;
    88	end;
    89	$$;
    90	
    91	comment on function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(text, text, text, text, text, boolean, integer, boolean, uuid) is
    92	  'T10.10: INSERT-eller-UPDATE felt-definition. key + pii_level (direct→non-direct) immutable for eksisterende (V3 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL). UPDATE rør ikke is_active (V8). pii_level escalation none→indirect→direct tilladt. Sikkerheds-invariants bypasses ikke for superadmin.';
    93	
    94	revoke all on function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(text, text, text, text, text, boolean, integer, boolean, uuid) from public, anon;
    95	grant execute on function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(text, text, text, text, text, boolean, integer, boolean, uuid) to authenticated;
    96

   100	  p_is_active boolean,

codex
De to tidligere build-fund ser ud til at være forsøgt lukket: audit-PII-assertionen er tilbage, og active-check-testen har nu flere wrapper/apply-dispatch-stier. Jeg gennemgår nu selve SQL-implementeringen for resterende kritiske fejl i write-vejene, ikke kun testdækningen.

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba supabase/migrations/20260521000004_t10_audit_filter_values.sql | sed -n '1,260p'" in /home/mathias/stork-2.0
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- Trin 10 T10.5: omskrive core_compliance.audit_filter_values med clients-fields-jsonb-walking
     2	--
     3	-- T1's audit_filter_values (20260514120006:9-86) walker kun top-level kolonner og
     4	-- hashes pii_level='direct'. Trin 10 udvider med special-case for core_identity.clients:
     5	-- walker fields-jsonb-keys og hashes hver key der har pii_level='direct' i
     6	-- client_field_definitions.
     7	--
     8	-- V2-fix (Codex V1 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): INGEN is_active-filter på direct-PII keys.
     9	-- Hashes alle direct-PII definitioner uanset is_active for at undgå datalæk når
    10	-- felt deaktiveres med eksisterende værdier stadig i clients.fields.
    11	--
    12	-- STABLE SECURITY DEFINER + set search_path = '' (matcher T1-pattern).
    13	-- Resten af T1-logik bevares uændret (top-level walking + unclassified-check).
    14	
    15	create or replace function core_compliance.audit_filter_values(
    16	  p_schema text,
    17	  p_table text,
    18	  p_values jsonb
    19	)
    20	returns jsonb
    21	language plpgsql stable security definer set search_path = ''
    22	as $$
    23	declare
    24	  v_result jsonb := p_values;
    25	  v_def record;
    26	  v_strict boolean := current_setting('stork.audit_filter_strict', true) = 'true';
    27	  v_has_defs boolean;
    28	  v_key text;
    29	  v_fields jsonb;
    30	  v_field_key text;
    31	  v_field_value jsonb;
    32	begin
    33	  if p_values is null then
    34	    return null;
    35	  end if;
    36	
    37	  -- Tjek om tabellen har klassificering.
    38	  select exists (
    39	    select 1 from core_compliance.data_field_definitions
    40	    where table_schema = p_schema and table_name = p_table
    41	  ) into v_has_defs;
    42	
    43	  if not v_has_defs then
    44	    if v_strict then
    45	      raise exception 'audit_filter_values: ingen klassificering for %.%', p_schema, p_table
    46	        using errcode = 'P0001';
    47	    else
    48	      raise warning 'audit_filter_values: ingen klassificering for %.% — værdier bevaret uændret', p_schema, p_table;
    49	      return p_values;
    50	    end if;
    51	  end if;
    52	
    53	  -- Walker top-level kolonner og hashes direct-PII (uændret T1-logik).
    54	  for v_def in
    55	    select column_name, pii_level
    56	    from core_compliance.data_field_definitions
    57	    where table_schema = p_schema and table_name = p_table
    58	  loop
    59	    if p_values ? v_def.column_name then
    60	      if v_def.pii_level = 'direct' then
    61	        -- BUG-FIX (V12 post-build): skip NULL-værdier. jsonb_set med NULL-value
    62	        -- returnerer hele jsonb som NULL → silent audit-data-tab. Matcher pattern
    63	        -- fra clients-special-case nedenfor (jsonb_typeof distinct from 'null').
    64	        if jsonb_typeof(p_values -> v_def.column_name) is distinct from 'null' then
    65	          v_result := jsonb_set(
    66	            v_result,
    67	            array[v_def.column_name],
    68	            to_jsonb(
    69	              'sha256:' ||
    70	              encode(extensions.digest((p_values->>v_def.column_name)::text, 'sha256'), 'hex')
    71	            )
    72	          );
    73	        end if;
    74	      end if;
    75	    end if;
    76	  end loop;
    77	
    78	  -- Trin 10 clients-special-case: walker clients.fields jsonb og hashes direct-PII keys
    79	  -- pr. client_field_definitions. V2 (Codex V1 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): hashes
    80	  -- ALLE direct-PII definitioner, uafhængigt af is_active — ellers ville deaktivering
    81	  -- af et felt skabe datalæk for værdier der allerede ligger i eksisterende fields.
    82	  -- T10.1's clients_fields_is_object-CHECK garanterer at fields er object her,
    83	  -- men defensiv jsonb_typeof-tjek bevares.
    84	  if p_schema = 'core_identity'
    85	     and p_table = 'clients'
    86	     and v_result ? 'fields'
    87	     and jsonb_typeof(v_result -> 'fields') = 'object' then
    88	    v_fields := v_result -> 'fields';
    89	    for v_field_key in
    90	      select key from core_identity.client_field_definitions
    91	      where pii_level = 'direct'
    92	    loop
    93	      if v_fields ? v_field_key then
    94	        v_field_value := v_fields -> v_field_key;
    95	        if jsonb_typeof(v_field_value) is distinct from 'null' then
    96	          v_fields := jsonb_set(
    97	            v_fields,
    98	            array[v_field_key],
    99	            to_jsonb('sha256:' || encode(extensions.digest(v_field_value::text, 'sha256'), 'hex'))
   100	          );
   101	        end if;
   102	      end if;
   103	    end loop;
   104	    v_result := jsonb_set(v_result, array['fields'], v_fields);
   105	  end if;
   106	
   107	  -- Tjek for ukendte kolonner (uændret T1-logik).
   108	  for v_key in select jsonb_object_keys(p_values) loop
   109	    if not exists (
   110	      select 1 from core_compliance.data_field_definitions d
   111	      where d.table_schema = p_schema
   112	        and d.table_name = p_table
   113	        and d.column_name = v_key
   114	    ) then
   115	      if v_strict then
   116	        raise exception 'audit_filter_values: ukendt kolonne %.%.% i input', p_schema, p_table, v_key
   117	          using errcode = 'P0001';
   118	      else
   119	        raise warning 'audit_filter_values: ukendt kolonne %.%.% — værdi bevaret uændret', p_schema, p_table, v_key;
   120	      end if;
   121	    end if;
   122	  end loop;
   123	
   124	  return v_result;
   125	end;
   126	$$;
   127	
   128	comment on function core_compliance.audit_filter_values(text, text, jsonb) is
   129	  'T10.5 (V2 Codex V1 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): T1-logik + core_identity.clients-special-case (jsonb-walking af fields for direct-PII keys pr. client_field_definitions; INGEN is_active-filter for at undgå datalæk ved felt-deaktivering). LENIENT-default; strict via stork.audit_filter_strict.';

     1	-- Trin 10 T10.12: read-RPC'er for klient + felt-definitioner
     2	--
     3	-- client_get: hent én klient med metadata (has_logo bool — logo hentes via
     4	--             dedikeret client_logo_get for at undgå unødigt bytea-payload).
     5	-- client_list: list alle klienter (aktive + inaktive per krav-dok §3.1).

     8	-- Tab-aware has_permission ('manage', false) per V6-fix: null-tab matcher
     9	-- ikke T10.13's tab-grants. SECURITY INVOKER — caller's role + RLS-policy gælder.

    11	create or replace function core_identity.client_get(p_client_id uuid)
    12	returns table (
    13	  id uuid,
    14	  name text,
    15	  fields jsonb,
    16	  is_active boolean,
    17	  logo_content_type text,
    18	  logo_filename text,
    19	  has_logo boolean,
    20	  created_at timestamptz,
    21	  updated_at timestamptz
    22	) language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
    23	as $$

    35	end; $$;

    43	-- ─── client_list: alle klienter (aktive + inaktive per krav-dok §3.1) ───

    45	returns table (
    46	  id uuid, name text, is_active boolean,
    47	  has_logo boolean, created_at timestamptz, updated_at timestamptz
    48	) language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
    49	as $$

    57	      from core_identity.clients c
    58	     order by c.name asc;
    59	end; $$;

    80	  end if;

    82	    select * from core_identity.client_field_definitions
    83	     where p_include_inactive or is_active = true
    84	     order by display_order, key;
    85	end; $$;

    12	create or replace function core_identity.client_logo_set(
    13	  p_client_id uuid,
    14	  p_logo_bytes bytea,
    15	  p_logo_content_type text,

    21	begin

    24	  end if;
    25	  if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
    26	    raise exception 'client_logo_set: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
    27	  end if;
    28	  if p_logo_bytes is null or p_logo_content_type is null or p_logo_filename is null then

    41	  if not found then
    42	    raise exception 'client_logo_set: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
    43	  end if;
    44	end;
    45	$$;

    54	) returns void

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba supabase/migrations/20260518000010_t9_seed_owners.sql | sed -n '1,130p'" in /home/mathias/stork-2.0
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- Trin 9 / §4 trin 9 Step 12: Seed Cph Sales + Ejere + Mathias/Kasper + superadmin-grants.
     2	--
     3	-- Plan V6 Valg 12 (V5-sweep): identity + version pair-pattern.
     4	-- mathias-afgoerelser pkt 1+18 + krav-dok 3.3.4: Mathias + Kasper på "Ejere"-afdeling.
     5	-- Eneste konkrete navne i krav-dokumentet (bootstrap, ikke fri valg).
     6	
     7	-- ─── FIX: has_permission record-syntaks-bug fra Step 11 (000009) ───────
     8	-- Step 11 deklarerede `v_grant record` og brugte `SELECT INTO v_grant.field`
     9	-- — Postgres tillader ikke INTO af individuelle record-felter før recorden
    10	-- som helhed er assigned. Manifesterede sig først ved DB-test af has_permission
    11	-- (record "v_grant" is not assigned yet, sqlstate 55000).
    12	--
    13	-- Step 11 er applied; immutability gælder. Fix via CREATE OR REPLACE her
    14	-- med individuelle bool-variabler i stedet for record.
    15	create or replace function core_identity.has_permission(
    16	  p_page_key text,
    17	  p_tab_key text default null,
    18	  p_can_edit boolean default false
    19	) returns boolean
    20	language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
    21	as $hp$
    22	declare
    23	  v_employee_id uuid;
    24	  v_role_id uuid;
    25	  v_can_access boolean;
    26	  v_can_write boolean;
    27	begin
    28	  v_employee_id := core_identity.current_employee_id();
    29	  if v_employee_id is null then return false; end if;
    30	
    31	  select role_id into v_role_id from core_identity.employees where id = v_employee_id;
    32	  if v_role_id is null then return false; end if;
    33	
    34	  -- Ny model: resolve via grants (tab → page → area).
    35	  if p_tab_key is not null then
    36	    select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    37	    from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    38	    join core_identity.permission_tabs t on t.id = g.tab_id
    39	    join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = t.page_id
    40	    where g.role_id = v_role_id
    41	      and p.name = p_page_key
    42	      and t.name = p_tab_key
    43	    limit 1;
    44	    if found then
    45	      return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    46	    end if;
    47	  end if;
    48	
    49	  -- Fald tilbage til page-niveau.
    50	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    51	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    52	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = g.page_id
    53	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
    54	  limit 1;
    55	  if found then
    56	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    57	  end if;
    58	
    59	  -- Fald tilbage til area-niveau (via page-name → area).
    60	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    61	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    62	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = g.area_id
    63	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.area_id = a.id
    64	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
    65	  limit 1;
    66	  if found then
    67	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    68	  end if;
    69	
    70	  -- Fallback til legacy role_page_permissions.
    71	  select can_view, can_edit into v_can_access, v_can_write
    72	  from core_identity.role_page_permissions
    73	  where role_id = v_role_id
    74	    and page_key = p_page_key
    75	    and (p_tab_key is null or tab_key = p_tab_key or tab_key is null)
    76	  order by case when tab_key = p_tab_key then 1 else 2 end
    77	  limit 1;
    78	
    79	  if found then
    80	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    81	  end if;
    82	
    83	  return false;
    84	end;
    85	$hp$;
    86	
    87	-- ─── FIX: closure-rebuild CTE-bug fra Step 3 (000002) ──────────────────
    88	-- Step 3's rekursive CTE havde `join n.node_id = ac.descendant_id` (linje 71)
    89	-- i stedet for `ac.ancestor_id`. Det fik recursion til at gen-besøge samme
    90	-- (parent, child)-relation på alle depths 1..100 i stedet for at gå op til
    91	-- bedsteforælderen. PK = (ancestor_id, descendant_id) → duplicate-key
    92	-- violation ved første ægte INSERT (her i seed_owners).
    93	--
    94	-- Step 3 er applied; immutability gælder. Fix via CREATE OR REPLACE her
    95	-- (PRE-seeds så closure-trigger har korrekt logik når seeds INSERT'er).
    96	create or replace function core_identity._org_node_closure_rebuild()
    97	returns void
    98	language plpgsql
    99	security definer
   100	set search_path = ''
   101	as $fix$
   102	begin
   103	  delete from core_identity.org_node_closure;
   104	
   105	  with recursive nodes_now as (
   106	    select distinct on (node_id) node_id, parent_id
   107	    from core_identity.org_node_versions
   108	    where effective_from <= current_date
   109	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > current_date)
   110	    order by node_id, effective_from desc
   111	  ),
   112	  ancestor_chain as (
   113	    -- Base: self-reference (depth=0).
   114	    select n.node_id as ancestor_id, n.node_id as descendant_id, 0 as depth
   115	    from nodes_now n
   116	    union all
   117	    -- Recursive: walk parent-chain (FIX: join på ancestor_id, ikke descendant_id).
   118	    select n.parent_id as ancestor_id, ac.descendant_id, ac.depth + 1
   119	    from ancestor_chain ac
   120	    join nodes_now n on n.node_id = ac.ancestor_id
   121	    where n.parent_id is not null
   122	      and ac.depth < 100
   123	  )
   124	  insert into core_identity.org_node_closure (ancestor_id, descendant_id, depth)
   125	  select ancestor_id, descendant_id, depth from ancestor_chain;
   126	end;
   127	$fix$;
   128	
   129	do $seed$
   130	declare

     4	-- role_page_permissions for admin-permission-rækker. Konfig-tabel definerer
     5	-- minimum N (default: 2) medarbejdere der bevarer admin-permission."

     7	-- Mekanik: AFTER-trigger på employees + role_page_permissions tjekker antal

    41	  for update to authenticated
    42	  using (current_setting('stork.allow_superadmin_settings_write', true) = 'true')

    53	  for each row execute function core_compliance.stork_audit();
    54	
    55	-- ─── enforce_admin_floor() — fælles helper-funktion ──────────────────────
    56	create or replace function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor()
    57	returns trigger
    58	language plpgsql
    59	security definer
    60	set search_path = ''
    61	as $$
    62	declare
    63	  v_active_admins integer;
    64	  v_min_admins integer;
    65	begin
    66	  select min_admin_count into v_min_admins
    67	    from core_compliance.superadmin_settings where id = 1;
    68	
    69	  select count(*) into v_active_admins
    70	    from core_identity.employees e
    71	    join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id
    72	   where e.anonymized_at is null
    73	     and p.page_key = 'system'
    74	     and p.tab_key = 'manage'
    75	     and p.scope = 'all'
    76	     and p.can_edit = true;
    77	
    78	  if v_active_admins < v_min_admins then
    79	    raise exception 'superadmin-floor overtrådt: % aktive admins er under minimum %', v_active_admins, v_min_admins
    80	      using errcode = 'P0001',
    81	            hint = 'Mindst ' || v_min_admins || ' admin-medarbejdere skal bevares. Tilføj ny admin før denne ændring.';
    82	  end if;
    83	
    84	  return null;  -- AFTER-trigger
    85	end;
    86	$$;
    87	
    88	comment on function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor() is
    89	  'AFTER-trigger der validerer at antal aktive admins er ≥ superadmin_settings.min_admin_count. Anvendes på employees og role_page_permissions.';
    90	
    91	-- ─── Trigger på employees: enforce ved UPDATE af role_id eller anonymized_at, og ved DELETE ──
    92	create trigger employees_enforce_admin_floor
    93	  after update of role_id, anonymized_at or delete on core_identity.employees
    94	  for each row execute function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor();
    95	
    96	-- ─── Trigger på role_page_permissions: enforce ved ALL mutations ─────────
    97	-- Permission-ændring kan reducere admins (eks. ændre scope fra 'all' til 'team').
    98	create trigger role_page_permissions_enforce_admin_floor
    99	  after update or delete on core_identity.role_page_permissions
   100	  for each row execute function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor();
   101	
   102	-- ─── Trigger på roles: enforce ved DELETE (kan fjerne admin-rolle helt) ──
   103	create trigger roles_enforce_admin_floor
   104	  after delete on core_identity.roles
   105	  for each row execute function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor();

     1	-- Trin 1 / fundament — DROP fase 0-tabeller fra public-schemaet.
     2	--
     3	-- Baggrund: Fase 0 (C1-D7) byggede 17 tabeller direkte i public. Master-planens
     4	-- rettelse 17 låste schema-grænser fra trin 1. Rettelse 18-20 har ændret design
     5	-- nok til at ALTER TABLE SET SCHEMA ikke ville være nok — strukturen skal
     6	-- genskabes i core_*-schemas med ny model (partitionering, anonymization_state,
     7	-- break_glass_requests, closure-table mfl.).
     8	--
     9	-- Mathias har godkendt drop-CASCADE (rettelse 20-eksekvering B2(a)).
    10	--
    11	-- Fase 0-data der mistes:
    12	--  - audit_log (188 rows): historik fra fase 0-bygning, ikke produktion
    13	--  - data_field_definitions (143 rows): seedes igen via classification.json
    14	--  - employees mg@ + km@: genskabes i bootstrap-step (t1_08)
    15	--  - pay_periods (auto-genereret af cron): genskabes ved trin 7-bygning
    16	--  - Test-rows i clients/org_units/teams/employee_teams/client_teams: ikke produktion
    17	--
    18	-- Cron-jobs droppes også — genskabes med ny schema-tilhørsforhold.
    19	
    20	-- Cron-jobs først (de refererer public-funktioner).
    21	do $$
    22	declare
    23	  v_job record;
    24	begin
    25	  for v_job in select jobname from cron.job loop
    26	    perform cron.unschedule(v_job.jobname);
    27	  end loop;
    28	end;
    29	$$;

     1	-- Trin 10 T10.6: clients_validate_fields BEFORE INSERT/UPDATE-trigger
     2	--
     3	-- LENIENT-default: WARNING ved ukendte/inaktive keys i fields jsonb.
     4	-- Strict-mode: stork.clients_fields_strict='true' → raise exception.
     5	--
     6	-- Matcher D5's pattern (genskabt i nyt schema). Inaktive felt-definitioner
     7	-- behandles som "ukendt" — keys i fields jsonb der refererer dem giver warning.
     8	-- Det er forretningsmæssigt korrekt: deaktiveret felt skal ikke længere udfyldes.
     9	--
    10	-- T10.16 tilføjer denne funktion til LEGACY_IS_ACTIVE_EXEMPT_FUNCTIONS-allowlist
    11	-- (Codex runde 7 KRITISK): client_field_definitions har kun is_active, ingen
    12	-- status-kolonne; R7d-pattern gælder ikke.
    13	
    14	create or replace function core_identity.clients_validate_fields()
    15	returns trigger
    16	language plpgsql stable security definer set search_path = ''
    17	as $$
    18	declare
    19	  v_strict boolean;
    20	  v_unknown_keys text[];
    21	begin
    22	  if new.fields is null or jsonb_typeof(new.fields) <> 'object' then
    23	    return new;
    24	  end if;
    25	
    26	  v_strict := coalesce(
    27	    nullif(current_setting('stork.clients_fields_strict', true), ''),
    28	    'false'
    29	  ) = 'true';
    30	
    31	  select array_agg(n.key order by n.key)
    32	    into v_unknown_keys
    33	    from jsonb_each(new.fields) as n(key, value)
    34	    where not exists (
    35	      select 1 from core_identity.client_field_definitions cfd
    36	      where cfd.key = n.key and cfd.is_active = true
    37	    );
    38	
    39	  if v_unknown_keys is not null and array_length(v_unknown_keys, 1) > 0 then
    40	    if v_strict then
    41	      raise exception 'clients_validate_fields: ukendte/inaktive keys i fields: % (stork.clients_fields_strict=true)',
    42	        v_unknown_keys using errcode = '23514';
    43	    else
    44	      raise warning 'clients_validate_fields: ukendte/inaktive keys i fields (LENIENT - INSERT/UPDATE accepteret): %',
    45	        v_unknown_keys;
    46	    end if;
    47	  end if;
    48	
    49	  return new;
    50	end;
    51	$$;
    52	
    53	comment on function core_identity.clients_validate_fields() is
    54	  'T10.6: BEFORE INSERT/UPDATE-trigger på core_identity.clients. LENIENT-default WARNING ved ukendte/inaktive keys i fields. Strict via stork.clients_fields_strict=true. Filtrerer på cfd.is_active=true som lifecycle-signal (R7d-allowlist i T10.16).';
    55	
    56	create trigger clients_validate_fields
    57	  before insert or update on core_identity.clients
    58	  for each row execute function core_identity.clients_validate_fields();

   151	-- ─── CREATE OR REPLACE pending_change_apply: tilføj 2 cases ─────────────
   152	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_apply(
   153	  p_change_id uuid
   154	) returns void
   155	language plpgsql
   156	security definer
   157	set search_path = ''
   158	as $$
   159	declare
   160	  v_change record;
   161	begin
   162	  select * into v_change
   163	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   164	  where id = p_change_id
   165	  for update;
   166	
   167	  if not found then
   168	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   169	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   170	  end if;
   171	
   172	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   173	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_approved: status=%', v_change.status
   174	      using errcode = '22023';
   175	  end if;
   176	
   177	  if v_change.undo_deadline > now() then
   178	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   179	      using errcode = '22023',
   180	            hint = format('undo_deadline=%s, now=%s', v_change.undo_deadline, now());
   181	  end if;
   182	
   183	  if v_change.effective_from > current_date then
   184	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   185	      using errcode = '22023',
   186	            hint = format('effective_from=%s, current_date=%s', v_change.effective_from, current_date);
   187	  end if;
   188	
   189	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   190	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_apply', true);
   191	
   192	  case v_change.change_type
   193	    when 'org_node_upsert' then
   194	      perform core_identity._apply_org_node_upsert(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   195	    when 'org_node_deactivate' then
   196	      perform core_identity._apply_org_node_deactivate(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   197	    when 'employee_place' then
   198	      perform core_identity._apply_employee_place(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   199	    when 'employee_remove' then
   200	      perform core_identity._apply_employee_remove(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   201	    when 'team_close' then
   202	      perform core_identity._apply_team_close(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   203	    when 'client_place' then
   204	      perform core_identity._apply_client_place(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   205	    when 'client_close' then
   206	      perform core_identity._apply_client_close(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   207	    else
   208	      raise exception 'unknown_change_type: %', v_change.change_type
   209	        using errcode = '42883';
   210	  end case;
   211	
   212	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   213	  set status = 'applied',
   214	      applied_at = now(),
   215	      updated_at = now()
   216	  where id = p_change_id;
   217	end;
   218	$$;
   219	
   220	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) from public, anon;
   221	
   222	-- ─── Seed undo_settings ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

   256	-- pending_change_approve.
   257	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_undo(
   258	  p_change_id uuid
   259	) returns void
   260	language plpgsql
   261	security invoker
   262	set search_path = ''
   263	as $$
   264	declare
   265	  v_change record;
   266	  v_page_key text;
   267	begin
   268	  select * into v_change
   269	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   270	  where id = p_change_id
   271	  for update;
   272	
   273	  if not found then
   274	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   275	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   276	  end if;
   277	
   278	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   279	    raise exception 'pending_change_wrong_status: % (expected approved)', v_change.status
   280	      using errcode = '22023';
   281	  end if;
   282	
   283	  if v_change.undo_deadline <= now() then
   284	    raise exception 'undo_deadline_expired'
   285	      using errcode = '22023',
   286	            hint = format('deadline var %s', v_change.undo_deadline);
   287	  end if;
   288	
   289	  -- Dispatcher: samme mapping som pending_change_approve.
   290	  case v_change.change_type
   291	    when 'org_node_upsert'     then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   292	    when 'org_node_deactivate' then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   293	    when 'team_close'          then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   294	    when 'employee_place'      then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   295	    when 'employee_remove'     then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   296	    when 'client_place'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   297	    when 'client_close'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   298	    else
   299	      raise exception 'unknown_change_type for undo-gate: %', v_change.change_type
   300	        using errcode = '42883';
   301	  end case;
   302	
   303	  if not core_identity.has_permission(v_page_key, null, true) then
   304	    raise exception 'permission_denied: undo % kræver can_edit på %', v_change.change_type, v_page_key
   305	      using errcode = '42501';
   306	  end if;
   307	
   308	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   309	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   310	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_undo', true);
   311	
   312	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   313	  set status = 'undone',
   314	      undone_at = now(),
   315	      updated_at = now()
   316	  where id = p_change_id;
   317	end;
   318	$$;
   319	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_undo(uuid) from public, anon;
   320

   393	-- ─── Cron: pending_changes_apply_due ────────────────────────────────────
   394	-- Selection-filter: status='approved' AND undo_deadline <= now() AND effective_from <= current_date.
   395	-- For hver: kald pending_change_apply (som re-verificerer due-check — V6).
   396	select cron.schedule(
   397	  'pending_changes_apply_due',
   398	  '* * * * *',  -- hver minut
   399	  $cron$
   400	    do $cron_body$
   401	    declare
   402	      v_change_id uuid;
   403	      v_success integer := 0;
   404	      v_failure integer := 0;
   405	      v_started timestamptz := clock_timestamp();
   406	    begin
   407	      perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'cron', true);
   408	      perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_changes_apply_due cron', true);
   409	      for v_change_id in
   410	        select id from core_identity.pending_changes
   411	        where status = 'approved'
   412	          and undo_deadline <= now()
   413	          and effective_from <= current_date
   414	        order by approved_at
   415	        limit 100
   416	      loop
   417	        begin
   418	          perform core_identity.pending_change_apply(v_change_id);
   419	          v_success := v_success + 1;
   420	        exception when others then
   421	          v_failure := v_failure + 1;
   422	        end;
   423	      end loop;
   424

   270	
   271	comment on function core_identity.pending_change_undo(uuid) is
   272	  'T9 Step 1: ruller approved-row tilbage før undo_deadline. Efter deadline: exception.';
   273	
   274	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_undo(uuid) from public, anon;
   275	
   276	-- ─── RPC: pending_change_apply (CENTRAL APPLY-GATE — V6 Beslutning 15) ────
   277	-- V6 Codex KRITISK-fix: sikkerheds-grænsen for "ikke materialiser future-dated"
   278	-- sidder HER, ikke kun i cron-filter. ALLE apply-paths (cron, manuel admin, test)
   279	-- går gennem samme gate.
   280	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_apply(
   281	  p_change_id uuid
   282	) returns void
   283	language plpgsql
   284	security definer
   285	set search_path = ''
   286	as $$
   287	declare
   288	  v_change record;
   289	begin
   290	  select * into v_change
   291	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   292	  where id = p_change_id
   293	  for update;
   294	
   295	  if not found then
   296	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   297	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   298	  end if;
   299	
   300	  -- V6 central apply-gate: due-check.
   301	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   302	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_approved: status=%', v_change.status
   303	      using errcode = '22023';
   304	  end if;
   305	
   306	  if v_change.undo_deadline > now() then
   307	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   308	      using errcode = '22023',
   309	            hint = format('undo_deadline=%s, now=%s', v_change.undo_deadline, now());
   310	  end if;
   311	
   312	  if v_change.effective_from > current_date then
   313	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   314	      using errcode = '22023',
   315	            hint = format('effective_from=%s, current_date=%s', v_change.effective_from, current_date);
   316	  end if;
   317	
   318	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   319	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_apply', true);
   320	
   321	  -- Dispatcher: switch på change_type til intern handler.
   322	  -- Steps 2+4+5 udvider via CREATE OR REPLACE af denne funktion med rigtige
   323	  -- CASE WHEN-handlers. I Step 1 er der ingen handlers, så vi raiser direkte.
   324	  raise exception 'unknown_change_type: %', v_change.change_type
   325	    using errcode = '42883',
   326	          hint = 'Step 1 dispatcher har ingen handlers; Steps 2+4+5 udvider via CREATE OR REPLACE';
   327	
   328	  -- Når Steps 2+4+5 udvider CASE: mark applied her efter handler returnerer.
   329	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   330	  set status = 'applied',
   331	      applied_at = now(),
   332	      updated_at = now()
   333	  where id = p_change_id;
   334	end;
   335	$$;
   336	
   337	comment on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) is
   338	  'T9 Step 1: CENTRAL APPLY-GATE. V6 Beslutning 15. Verificerer due-check (status=approved AND undo_deadline <= now() AND effective_from <= current_date). Hvis ikke: RAISE not_yet_due. Dispatcher til intern handler. Eksekveres af cron eller manuelt af admin; ALLE paths gennem samme gate.';
   339	
   340	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) from public, anon;
   341

   343	create or replace function core_identity.undo_setting_update(
   344	  p_change_type text,

    57	-- ─── Team-only validering ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    58	create or replace function core_identity._client_placement_team_check()
    59	returns trigger
    60	language plpgsql
    61	security invoker
    62	set search_path = ''
    63	as $$
    64	begin
    65	  -- Verificér at node_id refererer til team-knude (current version).
    66	  if not exists (
    67	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
    68	    where node_id = new.node_id
    69	      and node_type = 'team'
    70	      and effective_from <= new.effective_from
    71	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > new.effective_from)
    72	  ) then
    73	    raise exception 'client_placement_node_not_team: % er ikke team-knude på effective_from %', new.node_id, new.effective_from
    74	      using errcode = 'P0001';
    75	  end if;
    76	
    77	  return new;
    78	end;
    79	$$;
    80	
    81	create trigger client_node_placements_team_only
    82	  before insert or update on core_identity.client_node_placements
    83	  for each row execute function core_identity._client_placement_team_check();
    84	
    85	-- ─── Apply-handlers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    86	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
    87	  p_payload jsonb,
    88	  p_pending_change_id uuid
    89	) returns void
    90	language plpgsql
    91	security definer
    92	set search_path = ''
    93	as $$
    94	declare
    95	  v_client_id uuid;
    96	  v_node_id uuid;
    97	  v_effective_from date;
    98	begin
    99	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   100	  v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   101	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   102	
   103	  if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   104	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   105	      using errcode = '22023';
   106	  end if;
   107	
   108	  -- Luk eventuel åben placement (flyt).
   109	  update core_identity.client_node_placements
   110	  set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   111	  where client_id = v_client_id and effective_to is null;
   112	
   113	  -- Åbn ny placement (trigger validerer team-only).
   114	  insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   115	    (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   116	  values
   117	    (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, null, p_pending_change_id);
   118	end;
   119	$$;
   120	
   121	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_place(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
