   124	  p_payload jsonb,
   125	  p_pending_change_id uuid

 succeeded in 0ms:
   284	-- ─── _apply_client_place (place-handler) ──────────────────────────────────
   285	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
   286	  p_payload jsonb,
   287	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   288	) returns void
   289	language plpgsql
   290	security definer
   291	set search_path = ''
   292	as $$
   293	declare
   294	  v_client_id uuid;
   295	  v_node_id uuid;
   296	  v_effective_from date;
   297	  v_active record;
   298	begin
   299	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   300	  v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   301	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   302	
   303	  if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   304	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   305	      using errcode = '22023';
   306	  end if;
   307	
   308	  -- Verificér node er team + aktiv på v_effective_from.
   309	  if not exists (
   310	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
   311	    where node_id = v_node_id
   312	      and node_type = 'team'
   313	      and is_active = true
   314	      and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   315	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   316	  ) then
   317	    raise exception 'client_placement_requires_active_team: %', v_node_id
   318	      using errcode = 'P0001';
   319	  end if;
   320	
   321	  select * into v_active
   322	  from core_identity.client_node_placements
   323	  where client_id = v_client_id
   324	    and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   325	    and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   326	  limit 1;
   327	
   328	  if not found then
   329	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   330	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   331	    select v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from,
   332	      (select min(effective_from) from core_identity.client_node_placements
   333	       where client_id = v_client_id and effective_from > v_effective_from),
   334	      p_pending_change_id;
   335	  elsif v_active.effective_from = v_effective_from then
   336	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   337	    set node_id = v_node_id,
   338	        created_by_pending_change_id = coalesce(p_pending_change_id, created_by_pending_change_id),
   339	        updated_at = now()
   340	    where id = v_active.id;
   341	  else
   342	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   343	    set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   344	    where id = v_active.id;
   345	
   346	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   347	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   348	    values
   349	      (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, v_active.effective_to, p_pending_change_id);
   350	  end if;
   351	end;
   352	$$;
   353	
   354	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_place(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
   355	
   356	-- ─── _apply_client_close (close-handler — placement-tabel) ────────────────
   357	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_close(
   358	  p_payload jsonb,
   359	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   360	) returns void
   361	language plpgsql
   362	security definer
   363	set search_path = ''
   364	as $$
   365	declare
   366	  v_client_id uuid;
   367	  v_effective_from date;
   368	  v_active record;
   369	begin
   370	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   371	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   372	
   373	  if v_client_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   374	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + effective_from required'
   375	      using errcode = '22023';
   376	  end if;
   377	
   378	  select * into v_active
   379	  from core_identity.client_node_placements
   380	  where client_id = v_client_id
   381	    and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   382	    and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   383	  limit 1;
   384	
   385	  if not found then
   386	    return;
   387	  elsif v_active.effective_from = v_effective_from then
   388	    delete from core_identity.client_node_placements where id = v_active.id;
   389	  elsif v_active.effective_to = v_effective_from then
   390	    return;
   391	  else
   392	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   393	    set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   394	    where id = v_active.id;
   395	  end if;
   396	end;
   397	$$;
   398	
   399	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_close(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
   400

   402	create or replace function core_identity._apply_org_node_upsert(

commit 8896322d2ceaa2682f588eda303163f96c79a0cb
Author: Mathias Grubak <mg@copenhagensales.dk>
Date:   Thu May 21 02:48:07 2026 +0200

    Trin 10 T10.13b: seed legacy role_page_permissions for M1-test compat
    
    T10.13 seedede kun grant-modellen. M1-permission-matrix-test scanner RPCs og verificerer legacy role_page_permissions-row pr. superadmin. Uden legacy-row fejler M1-test.
    
    V6 Code-validering #5 (kun grant-model) var fejlagtig vurdering: legacy fungerer som M1-test-target. Tilføjer legacy-rows for clients + client_field_definitions/manage. Senere kan legacy fjernes når M1-test refactores (G-nummer-kandidat).
    
    Applied til remote via MCP.
    
    Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

+-- Trin 10 T10.13b: seed legacy role_page_permissions for M1-test compatibility
+--
+-- T10.13 seeder kun grant-modellen (permission_pages + permission_tabs +
+-- role_permission_grants). M1-permission-matrix-test scanner alle RPCs der
+-- kalder has_permission(...) og verificerer at superadmin har row i legacy
+-- role_page_permissions-tabel. Uden legacy-row fejler M1-test.
+--
+-- Legacy-pattern bevares til M1-test passes; senere kan legacy-rows fjernes
+-- når M1-test refactores til at læse grant-modellen direkte (G-nummer-kandidat).
+
+select set_config('stork.source_type', 'migration', false);
+select set_config('stork.allow_role_page_permissions_write', 'true', false);
+select set_config('stork.change_reason',
+  'T10.13b: seed legacy role_page_permissions for clients + client_field_definitions (M1-test compat)', false);
+
+insert into core_identity.role_page_permissions
+  (role_id, page_key, tab_key, can_view, can_edit, scope)
+select (select id from core_identity.roles where name = 'superadmin'),
+       page_key, tab_key, can_view, can_edit, 'all'
+from (values
+  ('clients',                  'manage', true, true),
+  ('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true, true)
+) as perms(page_key, tab_key, can_view, can_edit)
+on conflict (role_id, page_key, coalesce(tab_key, '')) do nothing;

exec

PLAN-AFVIGELSE (KRITISK): `t10_client_active_check.sql` erstatter stadig godkendt T10.15 end-to-end-flow.

Fund: Testen dokumenterer “TEST-BEGRÆNSNING”, men T2 kalder `_apply_client_place` direkte, T3/T7 indsætter `pending_changes` manuelt, T8 er kun alias til T3, og T6 kører ikke eksplicit cron/no-auth-context. Dermed mangler obligatorisk eksempel-row gennem non-admin `client_node_place` → `pending_change_request` session-var → approve → `pending_change_apply` for flere T10.7b-write-veje. Niveau 1-prefix: manglende write-vej-tjek = KRITISK.

LØS: Brug eksisterende auth-backed employee i rollback-test med midlertidig non-admin rolle + `client_placements/manage` grant; håndter admin-floor med buffer-admin eller transaction-local setup.

WORKAROUND-INTRODUCERET: `20260521000013_t10_seed_legacy_permissions.sql`.

Fund: Plan V14 siger T10.13 seeder grant-modellen, ikke legacy `role_page_permissions`. Build tilføjer legacy rows for M1-test compatibility og kommenterer selv “senere kan legacy fjernes” som G-kandidat. Det er bevidst kvalitets-sænkning/plan-afvigelse i permission-fundamentet.

LØS: Enten opdatér godkendt plan + registrér konkret G-nummer, eller fjern migrationen og ret M1-testen til grant-modellen før approval.
